If you get deeper into astrology, you realize that only the Sun sign tells you almost nothing. It's the whole natal chart that can give you some clarity on a person's personality and behaviours, and we also must not forget about the environment, culture, people, situations, opportunities, etc., people grew up in and how the individual perceived and received all of it. All of that shapes us. Even twins, that are born from the same egg, on the same day, almost the same hour and minute & the same environments, are different individuals.  I would say the most important signs to check for relationship compatibility are signs in Ascendant (you need to know the hour of birth to get this one), Venus, Mars and also Moon. If you are interested, I suggest checking compatibility of your whole natal charts. But, of course, nothing is set in stone. I personally use astrology more for better understanding of myself and others rather than something that is set in stone and that's how it is. I like to learn about something that I maybe don't really see yet in myself. The sooner the better. I don't like to dismiss anything, but I also question everything. And do some deep diving and thinking.  It's also really fun to do it together with someone. So you can think about stuff you might never think about and you talk to each other about what it says and how much it actually applies to either of you. And get to know yourselves and each other better. No matter how much we think we know ourselves, there's always something more to learn.  I also like to check, for example, Chinese horoscope which gives you another perspective & if you combine the characteristics of each horoscope (in your sign), you can get even more wholesome picture of, well, yourself.  Ooo, and my Sun sign is also Gemini on the cusp of Taurus & I must say I realized there's a little bit of Taurus in me a long time ago (but I don't have Taurus anywhere in my chart - except the proximity in my Sun sign). Horoscopes aside, I think you are beautiful people (inside and out) and are awesome together! Your whole wedding and all the speeches were like in a fairy-tale - just...magical. Congratulations & I wish you both a lifetime of love, respect and support. Bless you ğŸ’œ
